 // 2^n_leading_bits\n    dense_bucket_.assign(num_buckets_, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(0));\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate hash of the element\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Split the hash into two parts\n  // First n_leading_bits determine the bucket index\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);\n\n  // The remaining bits after removing the first n_leading_bits\n  uint64_t remaining_bits = hash >> n_leading_bits_;\n\n  // Find the position of the first 1-bit from the right (rho - leading zero count + 1)\n  // If remaining_bits is 0, position is maximum\n  uint64_t leading_one_pos = 0;\n\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    // All remaining bits are 0, set position to maximum\n    // This represents infinite leading zeros\n    leading_one_pos = 64 - n_leading_bits_;\n  } else {\n    // Find the position of the first 1-bit from the right\n    for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64 - n_leading_bits_; ++i) {\n      if ((remaining_bits >> i) & 1ULL) {\n        // Add 1 to position only if n_leading_bits > 0\n        leading_one_pos = (n_leading_bits_ > 0) ? (i + 1) : i;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Encode the position using dense bucket (4 bits) and overflow bucket (3 bits)\n  // Dense bucket stores the lower 4 bits\n  uint64_t dense_val = leading_one_pos & 0xF;  // Lower 4 bits\n  uint64_t overflow_val = (leading_one_pos >> 4) & 0x7;  // Next 3 bits\n\n  // Update buckets with maximum value seen\n  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();\n  uint64_t current_overflow = (overflow_bucket_.count(bucket_idx) > 0 ? overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong() : 0);\n  uint64_t current_full_pos = (current_overflow << 4) | current_dense;\n  uint64_t new_full_pos = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;\n\n  if (new_full_pos > current_full_pos) {\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate the harmonic mean of 2^(-M[i])\n  double raw_estimate = 0.0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; ++i) {\n    // Get the full position value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0 ? overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong() : 0);\n    uint64_t full_pos = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;\n\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(full_pos));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = α_m * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[i]))\n  // where α_m = 0.79402 for our implementation\n  double alpha_m = CONSTANT;\n  double cardinality_estimate = alpha_m * num_buckets_ * num_buckets_ / raw_estimate;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(cardinality_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":712,"cache_read_input_tokens":101282,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":712},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a99cf2cc-f95d-4489-9200-a38db0bd6e06","uuid":"9893a34b-2000-4c7f-bc64-b74177a29918"}

overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong() : 0);\n  uint64_t current_full_pos = (current_overflow << 4) | current_dense;\n  uint64_t new_full_pos = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;\n\n  if (new_full_pos > current_full_pos) {\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_val);\n    overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_val);\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate the harmonic mean of 2^(-M[i])\n  double raw_estimate = 0.0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; ++i) {\n    // Get the full position value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = (overflow_bucket_.count(i) > 0 ? overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong() : 0);\n    uint64_t full_pos = (overflow_val << 4) | dense_val;\n\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(full_pos));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = α_m * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[i]))\n  // where α_m = 0.79402 for our implementation\n  double alpha_m = CONSTANT;\n  double cardinality_estimate = alpha_m * num_buckets_ * num_buckets_ / raw_estimate;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(cardinality_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":9,"oldLines":7,"newStart":9,"newLines":7,"lines":[" HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits)","     : cardinality_(0), n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {","   // Initialize the number of buckets and dense bucket array","-  if (n_leading_bits <= 0) {","+  if (n_leading_bits < 0) {","     num_buckets_ = 0;","     dense_bucket_.clear();","   } else {"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

i < num_buckets_; ++i) {\n    raw_estimate += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = α_m * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[i]))\n  // where α_m = 0.79402 for our implementation\n  double alpha_m = CONSTANT;\n  double cardinality_estimate = alpha_m * num_buckets_ * num_buckets_ / raw_estimate;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(cardinality_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":556,"cache_read_input_tokens":109779,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":556},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a99cf2cc-f95d-4489-9200-a38db0bd6e06","uuid":"62dfa969-29a1-43a2-b994-edb6daa15dcf"}
